2026-03-29T00:36:40.2540792Z [36;1m# The following logic implements the configuration priority described in the README:[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2541207Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2541383Z [36;1m# Inputs[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2541580Z [36;1m# Environment Variables[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2541823Z [36;1m# Config File[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2542035Z [36;1m# Defaults[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2542227Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2542624Z [36;1m# As noted above defaults are awkward to handle as GitHub Actions will inject those values as the input[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2543284Z [36;1m# if the caller doesn't provide them, thus if the input matches the default we don't set it as we[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2543942Z [36;1m# can't tell the difference.  Plus if we did set it when it was the default value then it could potentially[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2544678Z [36;1m# override an external environment variable, or something in the callers configuration file, which then wouldn't[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2545275Z [36;1m# match the configuration priority that is documented.[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2545610Z [36;1mset_env_var_if_provided() {[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2545869Z [36;1m  local var_name="$1"[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2546106Z [36;1m  local input_value="$2"[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2546354Z [36;1m  local default_value="$3"[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2546593Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2546872Z [36;1m  if [ -n "$input_value" ] && [ "$input_value" != "$default_value" ]; then[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2547340Z [36;1m    # If action was provided with explicit input by the caller set that[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2547856Z [36;1m    # Use printf %q to safely escape special characters and prevent command injection[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2548497Z [36;1m    printf 'export %s=%q\n' "$var_name" "$input_value" >> trivy_envs.txt[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2549090Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2549271Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2549441Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2549711Z [36;1m# Set environment variables, handling those with default values[0m
2026-03-29T00:36:40.2550272Z [36;1m# cf. https://aquasecurity.github.io/trivy/latest/docs/configuration/#environment-variables[0m
